# Auree Jewellery (https://www.aureejewellery.com)

> Auree was founded by Amelia in 2014 from a simple belief that beautiful jewellery shouldn’t be hidden away for special occasions - it should be worn and loved every day.

Known for our gold Russian Wedding Rings (made in England), colourful gemstones, meaningful Birthstone Collections and our beautiful Personalised Necklaces, engraved in London - this is jewellery that is made to last.

We use the highest quality, sustainably sourced sterling silver, gold vermeil and solid gold - all designed to travel through life with you.
